FNV PBR CLOSE TERRAIN VERTEX DECLARATION CONTRACT

Questions:
1. Where does the engine create or bind D3D vertex declarations for the draw path?
2. Do close-terrain candidates use D3DVERTEXELEMENT9 declarations or legacy FVF?
3. Which static declarations, if any, match NVR TerrainTemplate.hlsl inputs?
4. Which runtime functions must be instrumented if the declaration is generated dynamically?

NVR TerrainTemplate.hlsl expects POSITION, TANGENT, BINORMAL, NORMAL, TEXCOORD0, COLOR0, TEXCOORD1, and TEXCOORD2.
